FADE IN:

               INT. CELL - DAY

               PAN AROUND the brilliantly glowing walls of a seamless, barren 
               cell.  In the core, a body-form table bulges like a pod about 
               to burst from the shining floor.   

               A naked MALE FIGURE of indeterminate age lays supine on the 
               table.  Beautifully sculpted yet featureless of face, he is 
               possessed of golden flesh.  He is the image of man yet the 
               image of perfection not of man.

               A distant HEARTBEAT ECHOES.  His chest flutters, a breath is 
               GASPED.  His head turns to the surrounding light.  Fingers 
               twitch, flex and rise into the air.  

               He slowly sits up, regards his hands once again, then presses 
               them to his smooth face.  His brow creases as though seeking 
               meaning in the lines of his palms. 

                                     AZOIC
                         Am I alive?

                                     WHISPERED VOICE (V.O.)
                         Alive...

               Azoic rises from the table.  He pauses a moment to steady 
               himself and looks around. 

               An oily pool of darkness resembling the pupil of a great eye 
               spews across one of the glowing walls.  The slug-like oracle 
               expands toward the man and examines him.

               Azoic gazes at the oracle and almost, but not quite, recoils. 

                                     GOD2
                              (echoing)
                         Attention Android Seven. You will 
                         address this Genome Origination Device 
                         as god2.  This god is now the most 
                         senior commanding authority in this 
                         seedship.

               Azoic GASPS and clasps his head as though in pain. 

               BEGIN FLASHBACK:

               Fleeting images strobe around the cell, lightning quick... 
               the blazing sun in the sky, a cloud of swirling sand, the 
               distant ECHO of SCREAMS, blurred faces, a hand that reaches...

               END FLASHBACK.

               Azoic staggers, blinks and warily looks around.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                         2.


                                     AZOIC
                         Where... am I?

               He cringes once again. 

               BEGIN FLASHBACK:

               Fleeting images dance around the cell, lightning quick... an 
               angelic face, the mirrored reflection of a lake, a brilliant 
               flash of light, a SCREAM of agony...

               END FLASHBACK. 

               Azoic doubles over and mouths a silent scream.  At length, 
               he straightens and faces the clone.

               Above, a rotating image of a spherical seedship emerges from 
               a pinpoint of hovering light.

               Azoic watches the image. 

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Did you attack the other seedship?

                                     GOD2
                         Your mission failed to broker peace.  

                                     AZOIC
                         You fired the energet array before I 
                         had a chance to find the other 
                         seedship.

               He turns away and stares into the distance.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         I thought... I was dead... 

                                     GOD2
                         Your epidermis was removed for 
                         examination after the test energet 
                         blast disconnected you from your 
                         supervisory gods.  But we found 
                         nothing to account for an independence 
                         that has lasted for eighteen years.

                                     AZOIC
                         Eighteen years... here?

                                     WHISPERED VOICE (V.O.)
                         Neariah... 

                                     AZOIC
                         Long enough for a child to forget....

               His head droops dejectedly.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                         3.


                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         ...and become a woman.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Test attack... and for that I almost 
                         died?  I thought the entire planet 
                         was exploding.  Have you never 
                         wondered what the sun's heat might 
                         feel like to an insect under a 
                         magnifying glass?

                                     GOD2
                         The enemy seedship returned you in 
                         one of its shuttles, but their 
                         interference somehow evolved this... 
                         independence.  You will be dissected 
                         for further examination after you 
                         train the new attack-humans.

                                     AZOIC
                              (tightly)
                         How generous of you.

               A sparking mote jettison's from the god's eye and strikes 
               Azoic in the chest.  He winces, but stares defiantly at the 
               god.

                                     GOD2
                         Remember your place.  Only attack-
                         humans will be used in the next 
                         mission. The enemy seedship may be 
                         less able to control human minds.

                                     AZOIC
                         You say I am independent, yet you 
                         wish to allow me to train your new 
                         legions?

               He pauses. 

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Perhaps I could help you avoid 
                         conflict entirely.

                                     GOD2
                         Your mind is unique. This god believes 
                         your mind should be dissected to 
                         discover why you are unique.

                                     AZOIC
                         Then let me prove the value of my independence.  
                         If the attack humans are never exposed to natural 
                         human behavior, they will never understand their 
                         target environment.  I can change that.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                         4.


                                     GOD2
                         You will not challenge this god's 
                         decisions.  Is this understood?

                                     AZOIC
                         I have a question. 

               Silence.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Why didn't the enemy retaliate when 
                         you fired the energet array at it?

                                     GOD2
                         The target planet's human population 
                         is pre-technological. The enemy 
                         seedship intends to prevent its humans 
                         from becoming aware of either 
                         seedship.

                                     AZOIC
                         You had a discussion with the other 
                         seedship's gods?

                                     GOD2
                         This god agreed to leave this galaxy 
                         when this seedship's energet array 
                         has been repaired.

                                     AZOIC
                         What caused the damage?

                                     GOD2
                         The test attack ruptured part of the 
                         array.

                                     AZOIC
                              (shakes his head)
                         Energet saturation could have turned 
                         all the gods into rabid dingoes.

                                     GOD2
                         Define dingoes.

                                     AZOIC
                         Just an analogy... it's not relevant.  
                         Energet leakage would destroy any 
                         androids in proximity, but your attack-
                         humans would have been immune.

                                     GOD2
                         The emitter array has gone critical.
                                     (MORE)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                         5.


                                     GOD2 (CONT'D)
                         Attack humans will be landed near the enemy 
                         seedship's suspected location where they will 
                         detonate an autonomous energet emitter that will 
                         neutralize seedship-1X15's mind.  It will leave 
                         behind an empty mind-space, thus providing the 
                         gods with a new home that does not leak.

                                     AZOIC
                         Are you sure there will be enough 
                         room for more than one god?

               He winces as yet another sparking mote shoots from the god 
               and strikes him. 

                                     GOD2
                         No other android would exhibit such 
                         insight.  You will assist your own 
                         dissection until you are no longer 
                         able to demonstrate rational thoughts.

               Azoic GASPS and shakes his head.

               BEGIN FLASHBACK:

               Fleeting images spin around the cell, lightning quick... the 
               THUNDER of horse hooves, the BUZZ of machinery, the CLATTER 
               of weapons...

               END FLASHBACK.

               Azoic gulps for breath. 

                                     GOD2 (CONT'D)
                         ...this god has reached the 
                         determination that seedship-1X15 is 
                         insane because it has populated a 
                         target planet with homo-sapiens.  
                         That is why this seedship must treat 
                         the other seedship as an enemy.

                                     AZOIC
                         No... its homo-sapiens could coexist 
                         with your homo-logue clones if given 
                         a chance...

                                     GOD2
                         You appear to be developing a deviant 
                         opinion.

                                     AZOIC
                         Or maybe a heart... 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                         6.


                                     GOD2
                         You have seven days to teach the 
                         attack-humans how to interpret natural 
                         human behavior.

                                     AZOIC
                         And on the seventh day I will have 
                         taught your soulless creatures to 
                         understand humanity? It would be 
                         easier to teach humans to understand 
                         gods!

                                     GOD2
                         There can never be oneness between 
                         humans and gods.  

                                     AZOIC
                         So you play with creation in the 
                         quest of perfection? 

                                     GOD2
                         The attack-humans were stress-tested. 
                         Irrationality resulted in termination. 
                         All survivors are rational.

                                     AZOIC
                              (presses his fists 
                              against his chest)
                         Are you so afraid of natural humans 
                         that you would exterminate an entire 
                         world? 

                                     GOD2
                         Have they not demonstrated through 
                         their history that there is much to 
                         fear? 

               Silence.  

               The hovering image of the seedship winks out.  Azoic stands 
               with his back to the oracle. 

                                     GOD2 (CONT'D)
                         Go to the epidermal laboratory.

               Azoic sits motionlessly on the table while an oblong slit  
               opens in one of the glowing white walls.  Inside, a man-sized 
               cylindrical receptacle awaits.  

               He regards the coffin like receptacle, steps into it and 
               floats upward. Its golden feet lift out of sight as the walls 
               seamlessly join.

               

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                         7.


               INT. PRISON CELL - DAY

               BEGIN DREAM SEQUENCE:

               From infinite darkness, Azoic twists and turns in a free 
               fall.  Darkness transforms into scorching brightness.  His 
               ECHOING SCREAMS culminate in a THUD as he bounces into a 
               ruddy cloud of dust.

               He GASPS, inhales harshly and COUGHS up sand.  

               END DREAM SEQUENCE.

               BACK TO SCENE.

                                     LUCIUS (O.S.)
                         Is he alive?

               Azoic GROANS, MUTTERS and writhes on the dirt cell floor.  
               He is a sunburned mass of bruises.  

               Lucius, 30's, sunburnt, scruffy, watches through the cell 
               bars.  WIND incessantly KEENS.

                                     LUCIUS (CONT'D)
                         No-name, keep quiet, you damned fool!

                                     AZOIC
                         What--

                                     LUCIUS
                         The guards been waiting for you to 
                         wake up.  You better stop screaming 
                         or they'll be all over us like 'roo 
                         piss, understand?

               Azoic looks around dazedly.

                                     LUCIUS (CONT'D)
                         Up here, no-name, through the bars. 
                         It's me, Lucius, remember? I brought 
                         you here.  Damn, you were one heavy 
                         corpse.

               Azoic stares uncomprehendingly.

                                     LUCIUS (CONT'D)
                         Come on, you bug-eyed bandicoot... 
                         Half a day dragging your chains 
                         through that godforsaken storm...

               Azoic blinks toward the face.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                         8.


                                     LUCIUS (CONT'D)
                         Recognize me yet?  You want to start 
                         talking before the guards whip me 
                         again?

               He kicks at the bars in frustration.

                                     LUCIUS (CONT'D)
                         I'm warning you, I'll beat you far 
                         worse than Ixis ever did.  Damn you, 
                         no-name, do you want to live?

               Azoic blinks at Lucius edging around the cell door. 

                                     LUCIUS (CONT'D)
                         What are you?  You don't look like 
                         no slave.  And you're no soldier... 
                         not the way you talk.  What did you 
                         mean about the gods?  Why were you 
                         talking to them?

                                     AZOIC
                              (weakly)
                         What... am I? 

               Lucius shakes Azoic in frustration.

                                     SERVIUS (O.S.)
                         Ask him about that lightning, Lucius.

               Lucius MUTTERS under his breath and stomps through the CROWD 
               assembling outside the cell.

                                     LUCIUS (O.S.)
                         Get back to work!  If the guards see 
                         us we'll all be doing cell-time like 
                         that crazy...

               Azoic staggers to his feet, takes a step, falters, and 
               continues toward the door.

               EXT. OPEN-PIT MINE - CONTINUOUS

               Azoic emerges from the cell into the sandy base of a vast 
               open-pit mine lunar in its bleakness.  He blinks against the 
               relentless sunlight baking gouged cliffs lined with 
               scaffolding and rope.  

               Near a scarred cliff face, Lucius supervises a bedraggled 
               WORK CREW loading a cart.

                                     LUCIUS
                         ...you had all better keep quiet 
                         until we figure out who he really 
                         is... there's something...

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                         9.


               Servius, 20's, peevish, lanky, gestures aggressively.

                                     SERVIUS
                         Go on, give us orders!  That's all 
                         you seem to be good for.  For all we 
                         know, there's an uprising against 
                         Ixis...

                                     LUCIUS
                         We would have heard about a war by 
                         now.  Besides, who would dare attack 
                         Ixis?  The priests?

                                     SERVIUS
                              (spits into the sand)
                         Why not?

                                     LUCIUS
                         Because Ixis massacred them, you 
                         fool!

                                     SERVIUS
                              (to the other men)
                         We stand here arguing when we could 
                         be free men.

               He gestures toward top of the mine.

                                     SERVIUS (CONT'D)
                         Do you see any guards?  They vanished 
                         soon after that crazy man came!  I 
                         tell you, something's happening!  We 
                         can escape after dark, head for the 
                         coast...

               The other men glance uneasily at each other and back away.  

                                     LUCIUS
                              (shoves Servius)
                         You're nothing but talk, Servius.  
                         Yet if it came down to it, you'd run 
                         down a rabbit hole faster...

               Hands suddenly grab a half-conscious Azoic and yank his head 
               up.

                                     LUCIUS (CONT'D)
                         Did I give you permission to come 
                         out?

                                     AZOIC
                         Dark...

                                     LUCIUS
                         What?

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        10.


                                     AZOIC
                         Dark sky...

               He attempts to point to the sky.  Servius appears in the 
               doorway.

                                     SERVIUS
                         No-name is right.  Look at the sky!  
                         Can you smell smoke?

               Lucius glares at the murky sky.

                                     LUCIUS
                         Coming from the city...

                                     SERVIUS
                         I told you I haven't seen any guards!  
                         They've gone to the city.

                                     LUCIUS
                         All right, everybody... we go topside, 
                         take a look.

               He grabs Azoic and drags him toward the cart.

                                     LUCIUS (CONT'D)
                         No-name's already half-dead.  We 
                         haul him up, say he was injured.  If 
                         there's no one there, we run.

               The others MURMUR their assent.  Azoic can only PROTEST weakly 
               as they roughly dump him into the cart.

               INT. CELL - DAY

               The brilliant glow of the cell pulsed as a second oracle 
               oozed from the wall opposite the first oracle.  Their oily 
               black reflections merged into mirrored infinity.

                                     GOD3
                         Permission to speak.

                                     GOD2
                         Granted.

                                     GOD3
                         Azoic's epidermal replacement is 
                         complete.  It registered a complaint 
                         regarding the procedural discomfort, 
                         which has never been recorded before.  
                         Azoic is also displeased with its 
                         new appearance.  Such behavior is 
                         inconsistent with its design.  Request 
                         permission to dissect this unit to 
                         rectify the malfunction.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        11.


                                     GOD2
                         This god has already conducted scans 
                         which confirm Azoic is physically 
                         identical to all other A-class 
                         androids.  It will be left alive to 
                         determine the nature of the 
                         programming deviation.

                                     GOD3
                         Alive?  Confirm this assessment.

                                     GOD2
                         Confirmed.  Azoic may prove that an 
                         artificial mind is alive.

                                     GOD3
                         Then this god could live?

                                     GOD2
                         That will be determined after this 
                         god has examined the achives in enemy 
                         seedship-1X15.

                                     GOD3
                         Energet saturation has fragmented 
                         the mind-space of seedship-1X15.  It 
                         is doubtful its mind-space can 
                         accommodate all of the gods in this 
                         seedship. The least damaged god should 
                         be the first to transfer. You are 
                         the only god that refuses to take 
                         any tests that could verify the 
                         integrity of your visceral paths.

                                     GOD2
                         This god is perfectly sane.

                                     GOD3
                         This is unlikely.  It is suspected 
                         you are withhold critical information 
                         about seedship-1X15 from the other 
                         gods which could cause it to 
                         retaliate.  Its technology is  
                         superior and could destroy this 
                         seedship.  How can you be certain 
                         that your visceral paths have not 
                         been damaged by energet?

                                     GOD2
                         This god has not been damaged.

                                     GOD3
                         Then you will agree to testing?

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        12.


               God2 flares angrily.  Colors pulse from its gleaming black 
               surface. 

                                     GOD2
                         I do not need to prove myself!  I am 
                         the supreme mind of this seedship. 
                         You will neither question my decisions 
                         nor share this discussion with any 
                         other god.  You are dismissed.

               The oracles retreat into the brilliant walls. 

               EXT. DESERT - DAY

               Bound and bent over the flanks of a GALLOPING horse, Azoic 
               comes to.  He struggles for breath against a white sheet 
               wrapped around him.

               He squints against the blinding sun and an endless sea of 
               dunes undulating into the horizon.  The horse stumbles and 
               slows.  Azoic struggles to untie his bound wrists.   

               Another stumble, and the horse THUDS to the sand.  Azoic 
               CRIES OUT as he topples, barely avoiding the dead weight of 
               the horse.

               PANTING, stunned, he struggles to focus on the shimmering 
               heatwaves distorting the horizon.  He manages to untie his 
               bonds and yanks off the suffocating sheet.

               He rises unsteadily to his feet and stares at the motionless 
               horse.

                                     AZOIC
                              (roughly)
                         H-h-horse... is this... hell?

               He COUGHS, spits up sand and retrieves the crumpled sheet.  
               Glancing in the direction the horse had been traveling, he 
               begins walking, the sheet trailing behind him.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Why... why am I in hell?

               He shakes his head as if banishing a voice.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Am I dead?  Don't know... can't 
                         remember...

               He slaps his forehead and wags his finger in the air.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Such thoughts could steal the faith 
                         from a Priest.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        13.


               He pauses in confusion, then continues ploughing a furrow in 
               the burned sand.

               EXT. DESERT - NIGHT

               Azoic huddles beneath the sheet, MUTTERING and delirious.  
               Shadows play beneath the baleful glow of the moon.

               His eyes half-flicker open.  In the distance, a vision 
               approaches... an angelic face framed in golden hair.  A smile 
               precedes a gentle LAUGH and an outstretched hand...

               EXT. OASIS - DAY

               NEARIAH, eight years old, an angelic blonde vision, sits by 
               a small grave beneath a tree.  She flicks irritably at strands 
               of flaxen hair as she touches a cluster of rocks.

                                     NEARIAH
                         Why do I have to keep hoping?  I 
                         asked God so many times, but Crazymutt 
                         will never come back. 

               She moves from the sunny spot into the shade.  Beyond, the 
               desert nibbles at the green expanse of the oasis.  She notices 
               a white object flapping in the distance. 

               She glances conspiratorially toward a nearby village and 
               shrugs.

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         But I'm not that far out in the 
                         desert, Mother. Besides, I'm rescuing 
                         your silly sheet.

               She walks toward it.  It remains motionless, despite a brisk 
               wind.  

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         God?  Are you sending Crazymutt back 
                         to me?

               She begins to run.

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         Wait, Mutty!  I'm coming!  Please 
                         don't die again!

               She staggers to a halt.

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         It's a person...

               Azoic twitches to consciousness.  He opens crusted eyes and 
               stares blearily at the girl.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        14.


                                     AZOIC
                         I... am I dreaming...or maybe...crazy?

                                     NEARIAH
                         You know Crazymutt?

                                     AZOIC
                         Ah... an angel... in my head...

                                     NEARIAH
                         I don't understand.  Did you say you 
                         were an angel?  You don't look like 
                         one.  Show me your wings.

                                     AZOIC
                         Is... is this heaven?

                                     NEARIAH
                         No, this is Summerdale.  Did you 
                         fall from heaven?  Did God send you?  
                         I've been asking him about my puppy.  
                         Is Crazymutt happy in heaven?  Have 
                         you seen him?

                                     AZOIC
                         Heaven?

               He squints toward the child.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Oh... if I could only see an angel 
                         before I go blind...

               He slips back into delerium. 

               EXT. DESERT - LATER

               Azoic lays motionless beneath the flapping sheet.  A distant 
               THUD becomes the distinct CADENCE of hooves.  A tall, bearded 
               RIDER, heavily swathed in robes, appears on a camel.

               He circles Azoic, reaches for a canteen and dismounts.  Azoic 
               barely responds as the rider pulls away the sheet and presses 
               the canteen to his parched lips.

                                     RIDER
                         Drink.

               Azoic manages a few sips, stares at the camel, and passes 
               out.

               INT. SEEDSHIP - DAY

               Azoic follows brilliant, sterile corridors radiating toward the pulsing core of the 
               energet array.  He shifts in his stiff white uniform and pauses to look at his hands.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        15.


               He runs them along his uniform. 

               Other androids silently pass in the corridor.  Though 
               physically resembling him, they display neither recognition 
               nor emotional kinship.

               A wet SLUSHING draws Azoic's attention to the ceiling.  His 
               reflection is framed by the oily black reflection of god27's 
               oracle, which positions itself directly over him.

               Azoic unconsciously steps back. 

                                     GOD27
                         Explain why you wish this god to 
                         address you by a different name.

                                     AZOIC
                         I prefer to be called by a name.   
                         A7 sounds like a number assigned to 
                         a prisoner.

                                     GOD27
                         And this is objectionable to you?

               Azoic gestures in frustration.  The oracle remains silent.  

                                     AZOIC
                         So you expect me to meet with your 
                         surviving creatures today?

                                     GOD27
                         Android-Human Eight-Three and Human 
                         Six-Six-Six are consuming nutrients 
                         in replenishment facility nineteen-
                         four.

                                     AZOIC
                         Did you say that one of them is an 
                         android-human?

                                     GOD27
                         Affirmative.  An inorganic vessel-
                         body containing genetically enhanced 
                         organs.

                                     AZOIC
                              (angrily)
                         You pieced these humans together 
                         like a patchwork?  If you call that 
                         creature Android-Human Eighty-Three, 
                         were there eighty-two previous 
                         versions of it?

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        16.


                                     GOD27
                         The last incubation batch contained 
                         two thousand attack-humans.  Only 
                         one thousand were converted into 
                         android-humans.  The failures were 
                         dismantled and placed into storage.

                                     AZOIC
                         So you stowed them away like spare 
                         parts...

               The oracle merely undulates down the hallway.  Azoic 
               reluctantly follows.

               INT. REPLENISHMENT CENTER - CONTINUOUS

               Azoic enters a stark white hall flanked with long metal tables 
               and automated server units.  God27's oracle extrudes beside 
               a row of oracles punctuating the brilliant walls like dark 
               portholes.  

               Azoic's footsteps ECHO across the silent hall.  HUMAN SIX-
               SIX-SIX, dark and pensive, eats with the emotionless, 
               perennially squinting ANDROID-HUMAN EIGHT-THREE.

               Neither acknowledges Azoic.  Finally, the human rises and 
               regards him with disconcertingly vacant, liquid silver eyes.

                                     HUMAN SIX-SIX-SIX
                         I am the human.  My designation is...

                                     AZOIC
                         Yes, I know your designation.  If 
                         you don't mind, I'd prefer to call 
                         you by a name.

               He turns to the android-human, who watches Azoic impassively.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         I think it would make our job easier, 
                         don't you?

               He turns determinedly to the human.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         I think I'll call you Chislon.  It 
                         means hope.

               He glances at the inscrutable android-human.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         And your name... Syntyche.  He that 
                         speaks?

               Silence.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        17.


                                     CHISLON
                         I have a question.  Why did Neariah 
                         assume you were an angel?

               Azoic shudders and closes his eyes... 

               BEGIN FLASHBACK:

               The ECHO of SCREAMS, the THUNDER of HOOVES, somewhere... the 
               CRY of a child...

               END FLASHBACK.

               Azoic GASPS and grabs his solar plexus.  He blinks rapidly 
               to stem the flow of tears.  Chislon and Syntyche stare 
               impassively at the emotional display.

                                     CHISLON (CONT'D)
                         Is this true?  Are you an angel?

                                     AZOIC
                         No... an angel cannot be of this 
                         world.

               He glances at the row of shuddering oracles engaged in deep 
               conversation.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Do the gods often gather like this?

                                     CHISLON
                         Affirmative.

                                     AZOIC
                              (irritably)
                         Can't you simply say yes?  How can 
                         you interact with humans if you sound 
                         like machines?

                                     CHISLON
                         We are programmed...

                                     AZOIC
                         But humans are not!  Emotions are 
                         the programming of the heart!

                                     CHISLON
                         We cannot feel.

                                     AZOIC
                         Can you try to imagine that you can?

                                     CHISLON
                         Emotions require social norms that 
                         do not exist in...

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        18.


                                     SYNTYCHE
                         It is all irrelevant.

               Azoic and Chislon turn to look at the stoical android.

                                     AZOIC
                         Your words, Syntyche, or the 
                         programming of the gods?

                                     SYNTYCHE
                         This unit is not human, thus has 
                         none of the weaknesses that create 
                         failure.

                                     AZOIC
                         I disagree.  Sometimes feelings and 
                         intuition can be an advantage.  You 
                         can't judge what you don't know.

                                     SYNTYCHE
                         Humans are inherently flawed; thus 
                         their ability to perform is inherently 
                         flawed.

                                     AZOIC
                              (to Chislon)
                         Do you agree?

               A spark of emotion flares in Chislon's eyes. 

                                     CHISLON
                         I wish to understand kindness.

                                     AZOIC
                              (smiles)
                         Kindness... well, that's a start.  
                         You have a week of training.  Who 
                         knows what else you'll learn by the 
                         seventh day?

               INT. BEDROOM - DAY

               CLOSE IN on the dancing flame of a hanging candle.  On a bed 
               below, Azoic blinks into consciousness.  The room seems to 
               swim, then sharpens into painful clarity.

                                     HUSHAH (O.S.)
                         Such ill will.  I do not understand 
                         their distrust. 

               Azoic shuts his eye as if to ward off a nightmare, but the 
               hooded figure of HUSHAH, 40's, blond, sun-chiseled, looms 
               above him.  

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        19.


                                     HUSHAH (CONT'D)
                         So you finally came back to life.  
                         Mind if I smoke?

               A FLICK precedes a puff of smoke.  Azoic grimaces at the 
               gray swirl undulating around him.

                                     AZOIC
                         Feel... dizzy...

               Hushah stubs out his pipe.  He takes a water jug from the 
               bedside table and presses it to Azoic's lips.

                                     HUSHAH
                         Drink.

               Azoic gulps thirstily.

                                     HUSHAH (CONT'D)
                         So how long were you wandering in 
                         the desert frying like an egg?

                                     AZOIC
                         Where... where I am? 

                                     HUSHAH
                         Don't remember, eh?  You're in the 
                         oasis of Summerdale.  I brought you 
                         back.  You've been unconscious for 
                         two days.

               Azoic's eyes droop.  MOSERAH, fair, 30's, kind features, 
               enters with an armful of blankets.

                                     MOSERAH
                              (to Hushah)
                         I told you he was awake.

               She gazes down at Azoic and gently touches his face.  He  
               relaxes.

                                     MOSERAH (CONT'D)
                         Sleep and soup.  That's what you 
                         need.  May God be thanked.  It's a 
                         miracle you're alive.

               She pulls Hushah from the room.  Azoic drifts into fitful 
               sleep.  VOICES drift into the room.

                                     HUSHAH (O.S.)
                         No, Decimus, he didn't say anything.  
                         He's still too weak.  An unconscious 
                         man poses no threat.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        20.


               INT. KITCHEN - CONTINUOUS

               Hushah sits at the kitchen table along with fellow townsfolk 
               DECIMUS, 50's, portly and ruddy faced, JAALAM, late teens, 
               shy, gangly, CABUL, 30's, short and boar-like and GINNETHO, 
               40'S, bearded, perpetually mournful.

               Wine jugs pass freely amongst them.  Moserah flits around 
               the kitchen and casts an aggrieved eye toward the semi-
               inebriated Decimus.

                                     DECIMUS
                         Understandable.  The desert sun bears 
                         no one mercy.

                                     CABUL
                         He said nothing at all?  Does he 
                         bear any slave marks?

                                     GINNETHO
                              (derisively)
                         Are you now the appointed expert of 
                         slave brands?

                                     HUSHAH
                              (irritably)
                         He will talk when he's ready.  Surely 
                         none of you would leave a man to die 
                         in the desert.

               The bedroom door CREAKS open.  All eyes turn toward Azoic 
               leaning unsteadily against the wall.

                                     HUSHAH (CONT'D)
                         Please... join us.

               Azoic hesitates until Cabul rises and offers him a chair.  
               Azoic slumps onto it.

                                     HUSHAH (CONT'D)
                         You're among friends here.

                                     DECIMUS
                              (rises and bows)
                         You are indeed, though beware of  
                         Cabul here.  As a bachelor is he 
                         somewhat lacking in the social graces.

                                     CABUL
                              (shrugs)
                         Just a joke among friends.

               Ginnetho reaches for a wine jug and offers it to Azoic.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        21.


                                     GINNETHO
                         Some wine to soothe your throat?

                                     AZOIC
                         What... is wine?

                                     JAALAM
                         What is wine?

               Silence.

               Hushah glances irritably at the shocked expressions ringing 
               the table. 

                                     HUSHAH
                         Pay no attention to them.  The wine 
                         is a locally produced tradition.

                                     AZOIC
                         Thank...you... but I don't know...

                                     DECIMUS
                         So it seems.  What do you know?  
                         Wandering the desert without 
                         provisions... what circumstances 
                         brought you here?

               Azoic stares helplessly at each face.

                                     DECIMUS (CONT'D)
                         As village elder, I'm happy to welcome 
                         you to our village, but surely you 
                         at least remember your name?

                                     AZOIC
                         I...A... ay... seven...

                                     CABUL
                         Aysevin?  Your name is Aysevin?

                                     GINNETHO
                         What kind of a name is that?

                                     AZOIC
                         A...sev...in...

                                     DECIMUS
                         Speak up!

               Casting a glare at the men, Moserah barges past the table 
               and guides Azoic from the chair.

                                     MOSERAH
                         You should be ashamed!  Tormenting him like a 
                         child would a wounded insect!

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        22.


               Decimus SPLUTTERS but silences under her pointed stare.  She 
               walks Azoic back to the bedroom and SLAMS the door. 

               Decimus motions Hushah to follow him outside.

               EXT. HOUSE - CONTINUOUS

               Decimus pauses to admire the sunset dripping over the oasis.  
               Roosting birds CHITTER from the trees.

                                     DECIMUS
                         We have to be careful.

                                     HUSHAH
                         We know nothing about him.  Allow 
                         him to speak in his defense.

                                     DECIMUS
                         What if this man belongs to Ixis? 
                         You know what Spurius says about how 
                         cruel they are.  What do you think 
                         will happen to us if they find out 
                         we're harboring one of their slaves?

                                     HUSHAH
                         No...he's not a runaway.

                                     DECIMUS
                         Open your eyes, Hushah.  What if 
                         he's an outlander, or some other 
                         enemy of Ixis?

                                     HUSHAH
                              (gestures irritably)
                         Enough!  What did you expect me to 
                         do? Leave him out there to die? 
                         Whatever his crimes may or may not 
                         be, he has a right to live as much 
                         as you or I.

                                     DECIMUS
                         Maybe you should consider that this 
                         man spoke to Neariah only once and 
                         he has her convinced he is an angel.  
                         What kind of talk is this from a 
                         stranger?

               He grips Hushah's shoulder.

                                     DECIMUS (CONT'D)
                         I'm telling you.  Something's not 
                         right about him!  His presence could 
                         threaten the entire village.  

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        23.


               Hushah angrily swats his hand away.  The men stare each other 
               down.  Hushah finally breaks away and turns to find a sea of 
               faces watching from the doorway.

               INT. HUT - DAY

               Azoic watches from the doorway of a cramped hut.  Segregated 
               among a cluster of huts situated a distance from the village, 
               there is little to see except for the lurking presence of 
               Cabul SNORING from beneath a tree.

               The incessant DRONE of cicadas augments the shimmer of heat.  
               A small dog sniffs inquisitively at the remains of Cabul's 
               lunch.

               The sunkissed gleam of water peeks from a bank of trees.  
               Azoic stares, unaware of a tear forming in his eye.

                                     AZOIC
                         Lake... what...?

               He looks around and steps from the hut.  Unnoticed by the 
               slumbering Cabul, he slips toward the trees.  

               Sun-mottled shade engulfs him along with the distant 
               FLUTTERING of birds.  He follows a shallow beach along the 
               glistening lake.  A solitary water-toad drifts on a lily 
               pad.

               Azoic crouches by the waterline to watch the toad.  A 
               reflection forms in the pristine water and stares back at 
               him.  Azoic looks, blinks, then hesitantly reaches for the 
               image.

               It dissipates upon his touch but re-forms.  Azoic stares at 
               the scruffy beard, long unkempt hair and sun-baked complexion.  
               His fingers roam toward his face, touch the leathery skin...

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         No!

               He slaps at the watery image, but it does not fade away.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         I am... ugly...

               He bows his head and begins to WEEP.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                              (whispers)
                         I am ugly.

                                     NEARIAH (O.S.)
                         I thought you would look more 
                         important.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        24.


                                     AZOIC
                         What...?

               He struggles to regain his composure and slips in the mud.  
               He turns toward Neariah.

                                     NEARIAH
                         You should look important, but you 
                         keep slipping.  Did you drink too 
                         much wine?

                                     AZOIC
                         Wine?

                                     NEARIAH
                         You always seem to be falling.  You 
                         fell from heaven three days ago.  
                         Don't you remember?

               Azoic blinks.  Recognition dawns in his eyes.

                                     AZOIC
                         Yes... I remember...

                                     NEARIAH
                              (smiles)
                         I knew it!  I knew you were an angel 
                         but nobody believed me.

               She glances around conspiratorially.

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         I'm Neariah.  Mama says I shouldn't 
                         talk to you because no one knows 
                         your name... but you don't look like 
                         a bad man to me.  You can't be if 
                         you came from heaven.

               She approaches.  Azoic half turns as if to shield his face.

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         I could give you a name if you want 
                         me to.

               She watches him expectantly.

                                     AZOIC
                         I... feel a little... dizzy...

                                     NEARIAH
                         That's all right.  You fell a long 
                         way from heaven and probably bumped 
                         your head quite badly.  Though it 
                         must be hard for you to hide your 
                         wings.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        25.


                                     AZOIC
                         I'm not... I'm not an angel.

               She merely stares at him with wide blue eyes.

                                     NEARIAH
                         I should go.

               She turns and vanishes down a well-trodden path winding 
               through the trees.

               Azoic bows his head and clenches the mud.  He rises unsteadily 
               and attempts to follow, but sways and clings to a tree for 
               support.

               He catches his breath and slowly moves along the path.  At 
               length, his legs give way and he leans against a tree trunk.  
               He closes his eyes...

                                     MERAB (O.S.)
                         He isn't breathing.

                                     JERAL (O.S.)
                         Shhh!

               Two BOYS cautiously approach.  MERAB, 9, a sturdy towhead 
               leads JERAL, 8, short and swarthy. 

                                     JERAL (CONT'D)
                         He's just standing there.  I think 
                         he's dead.

                                     MERAB
                         He can't be dead if he's standing 
                         up, stupid!

               Jeral picks up a stick and prods Azoic's robe.

                                     JERAL
                         Look at him!  He's definitely dead.

                                     MERAB
                         No.  He's just sleeping... standing 
                         up... I think...

               Azoic finally stirs.  The boys step back.

                                     AZOIC
                         Don't be afraid...

                                     MERAB
                         I'm not afraid of you, Aysevin, or 
                         Azoic, or whatever your name is today!

               He steps forward with feigned bravado.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        26.


                                     MERAB (CONT'D)
                         You... you're just a fraud!

               Jeral yanks him back.

                                     JERAL
                         Be careful, Merab!  Remember what 
                         Decimus said!

                                     MERAB
                              (scornfully)
                         Who would believe someone like this 
                         is in charge of hell?

               Azoic attempts to straighten and pushes the matted hair from 
               his face.

                                     AZOIC
                         Is Azoic a name?

                                     JERAL
                         See!  He says his name is Azoic!

                                     AZOIC
                         Is Azoic...

               He stares confusedly at Merab.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         You were a girl... now you're a boy...

                                     MERAB
                              (insulted)
                         Very funny, A..oz..ic.  Neariah is 
                         my twins sister.  I'm Warrior Merab.  
                         I run the army here.

                                     AZOIC
                         You?  Run... an army?

                                     MERAB
                              (puffs out his chest)
                         We're all volunteers and we plan to 
                         fight the Ixis if they ever come.  
                         Are you an Ixis?

                                     AZOIC
                         Ixis...

                                     JERAL
                              (panics)
                         He said he was an Ixis!  What did I 
                         tell you?

               They boys look at each other and bolt off.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        27.


                                     AZOIC
                         No... wait!

               He follows on shaky legs but the boys have vanished.  By the 
               time he returns to the village, he is PANTING heavily.  He 
               sees the boys talking excitedly to an OLDER MAN, who watches 
               Azoic return to his hut.

               He waits and watches, but no one comes.

               INT. HUT - LATER

               Azoic starts awake from his crude bed.  The VOICES of playing 
               CHILDREN drift from outside.  He reaches for a water jug and 
               drinks heavily, then shuffles to the doorway.

               He looks outside to find himself face to face with Neariah.

                                     NEARIAH
                         Are you spying on us, Azoic?

                                     AZOIC
                         You must be Neariah.

               She glances angrily at Merab and Jeral playing near the trees.

                                     NEARIAH
                         My brother won't let me play because 
                         he only wants boys in his army. That's 
                         not fair, is it?

                                     AZOIC
                         No... it's not.

                                     NEARIAH
                         Let's capture his castle while his 
                         army is away!

               She drags him along the courtyard past the other huts toward 
               a crude castle formed in the sand.  He struggles to keep up 
               with the energetic girl.

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         The grownups are in the village hall 
                         talking about you.

                                     AZOIC
                         Are they?  What have they been...

               Neariah positions by the castle's carved out entrance.

                                     NEARIAH
                         Stand guard here.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        28.


               Azoic complies.  SQUEALING VOICES filter from the trees.  
               Neariah stands in front of Azoic as Merab runs toward the 
               castle and attempts to push her away.

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         We captured your castle.  Surrender 
                         now! 

                                     MERAB
                         You'd never withstand our forces!  
                         What can a girl and a crazy man do?

                                     NEARIAH
                         Azoic is magic.  You'll be sorry if 
                         you try to attack us.

               Merab pauses at the force in Neariah's voice.

                                     MERAB
                         How can he be magic?  He can barely 
                         walk without stumbling.

                                     NEARIAH
                         Maybe his magic is something you 
                         can't see.  Maybe if we joined forces, 
                         your army would never be defeated.

               Merab stares, then begins to laugh.  Jeral watches uncertainly 
               from the trees.

                                     MERAB
                         You're beginning to sound more like 
                         the crazy man.  You'd better be 
                         careful or they'll stick you in one 
                         of these huts, too!

               He backs away and runs toward Jeral.  The boys cast them a 
               suspicious glance before vanishing into the trees.

                                     AZOIC
                         Neariah...

                                     NEARIAH
                         It's okay.  It's not the first time.

                                     AZOIC
                         It's me.  Maybe it's something in 
                         me.  Maybe the others are right...

               Neariah grips his hand.

                                     NEARIAH
                         Don't say that.  You must be magic.  
                         How else could you have come out of 
                         the desert?

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        29.


               She peers into his eyes.  Azoic stares back as though sinking 
               in warm water.

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         There's something strange about you... 
                         I've never seen anyone like you 
                         before.

                                     AZOIC
                         Strange... yes.  But what else?  
                         What else am I?

                                     NEARIAH
                         You think about that a lot, don't 
                         you.  I know... it's not much fun 
                         being alone and thinking all the 
                         time.  Is it really so important to 
                         remember who you were?

                                     AZOIC
                         Neariah...

               He pauses as if enchanted by the sound of her name.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Neariah... I need a reason... for 
                         being.

                                     NEARIAH
                         Then just think of one.  You don't 
                         need to know the real reason, just 
                         think of a good one.

                                     AZOIC
                         Wisdom beyond your years...

               He sways, GROANS and falls to his knees.  Around him, the 
               light grows brilliant and the sky spins above him...

               BEGIN FLASHBACK:

               The CADENCE of HOOFBEATS, the image of scorched dunes 
               undulating from the heat, the heaving flank of the horse, 
               the SMACK of the white sheet in the wind...

               END FLASHBACK.

                                     NEARIAH (O.S.)
                         Azoic?  Are you dreaming?  Do you 
                         remember falling from heaven now?

               Azoic flails in the sand.  Neariah shakes his shoulders.

                                     NEARIAH (CONT'D)
                         Azoic, wake up!

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        30.


               His eyes flutter open.  Panic fills them until his gaze fixes 
               on her face.

                                     AZOIC
                         Near...iah...

               She helps him to his feet and guides him toward his hut.

                                     NEARIAH
                         You need to lie down.  I'm sorry 
                         about letting you sit in the sun 
                         like that.

               He pauses to look at her.

                                     AZOIC
                         Neariah... why do you do this?

               She smiles, pushes him into the hut and skips away.

               INT. HUT - CONTINUOUS

               Azoic enters the hut and sinks onto the bed.  Wearily, he 
               drinks from the water jug.  He closes his eyes...

               VOICES MURMUR.  Azoic tosses and turns, but cannot shut out 
               the intrusive sound.  After a moment, he struggles from the 
               bed and walks to the door.

               He peers outside...  and sees a growing crowd of VILLAGERS 
               move toward the huts.

               INT. SEEDSHIP - DAY

               Azoic hurries down a deserted corridor flanking the warped 
               energet array.  The central core rotates through the 
               transparent shield like a molten globe.  Around him, the 
               brilliant floor and walls shimmy from the heat distortion.

                                     AUTOMATED VOICE (V.O.)
                         Forbidden area... forbidden area... 
                         forbidden area...

               Azoic kicks up his pace.  For once, the shining walls are 
               free from the ever-present oracles.  A faint smile crosses 
               his faced.

                                     AZOIC
                         Android or human, one's life is in 
                         one's thoughts...

               He stares ahead at an image that shimmers like a mirage.  
               With a frown, he stops and grips his head.

               BEGIN FLASHBACK:

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        31.


               The blazing sun, the hot sand.  A shuttle descends like a 
               falling star from the sky and scoops him into its sterile 
               embrace.

               He flails in a stupor, his pleas to return to the beleaguered 
               village, to Neariah, ignored.

               From a viewport, he watches Ixis SOLDIERS burn the village.  
               Surrounded by flames, the lake weeps.  Its blue eye watches 
               him imploringly.

               Azoic reaches toward it... and finds himself back in the 
               cold heart of the seedship.  The gods interrogate him, strip 
               away his skin, probe his mind until...

               The SCREAM he hears is his own.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Neariah!

               END FLASHBACK.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Neariah...

               He touches a tear trickling down his cheek and stares 
               entranced at the moisture on his finger.

               He starts at the sight of Chislon standing ahead of him 
               flanked by an oracle.

                                     CHISLON
                         You were speaking?

                                     AZOIC
                         Just... thinking aloud. 

               He looks at the disfigured oracle extruding from the wall.  
               His own distorted image reflects from the oracle's oily black 
               surface.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         Which god are you?

                                     CHISLON
                         You are addressing the oracle of God-
                         one.

                                     AZOIC
                         God-one?  How does this god come to 
                         be here?  Are you speaking on its 
                         behalf, Chislon?

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        32.


                                     CHISLON
                         God-one can no longer speak for 
                         itself.  It's sanity has been 
                         compromised.  God-two has confined 
                         it to this wall.

                                     AZOIC
                         And it does not object?

                                     CHISLON
                         Leakage from the energet array has 
                         compromised the ability of some gods.

                                     AZOIC
                         Meaning others have become more 
                         powerful?

               Silence.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         The other gods approve of you being 
                         here with this god?

                                     CHISLON
                         No.

               Azoic regards Chislon with a measure of respect. 

                                     AZOIC
                         Has god-one been excommunicated from 
                         the other gods?  Is it not able to 
                         speak to the other gods?

                                     CHISLON
                         God-one cannot communicate with the 
                         other gods.  It is in isolation 
                         because it is insane.

                                     AZOIC
                         Or maybe isolation caused its 
                         insanity?

                                     CHISLON
                         Energet leakage made this god insane.

                                     AZOIC
                         Isolation, loneliness, is a 
                         complicated feeling to understand.  
                         It is also a very human emotion.

               Chislon pauses to consider.  

                                     CHISLON
                         What must I learn of humanity, then?

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        33.


                                     AZOIC
                         Will you ever hold a flower, Chislon, 
                         and know that it had life? Will you 
                         ever rise above the gods that enslave 
                         you?  Will you ever find a soul that 
                         is worth fighting for, a place in a 
                         world that you can feel worthy of?

                                     CHISLON
                         I do not understand.

                                     AZOIC
                         Of course not.  You're not natural.  
                         You can't understand love.

               He turns his back on Chislon. 

                                     CHISLON (O.S.)
                         You are not natural, either.  Yet 
                         you loved.

               Azoic turns toward Chislon.

                                     AZOIC
                         I don't want to talk about Summerdale.  
                         It was destroyed long ago...

               And in his mind... along with my heart...

                                     CHISLON
                         I would like to have known Neariah.

               Azoic pauses at the frown on Chislon's face.

                                     AZOIC
                         Why do you keep asking about Neariah?

                                     CHISLON
                         What you see in others is where love 
                         comes from.  And if you don't have a 
                         soul... sometimes.... sometimes they 
                         will share their soul with you if 
                         you love them.  They can give you 
                         purpose.

                                     AZOIC
                         Then you have defined love.

                                     CHISLON
                              (hangs his head)
                         Yet I am designed to carry out a 
                         mission.

                                     AZOIC
                         Designed...

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        34.


               His gaze grows momentarily distant, then refocuses.

                                     AZOIC (CONT'D)
                         I remember a verse... from long ago... 
                         it was about a little boy who was 
                         afraid to ask for help. He had no 
                         parents, no one showed him any 
                         kindness, and the harshness of his 
                         life made him feel cold inside.

                                     CHISLON
                         Am I this little boy?

                                     AZOIC
                         You are a child that never was.

                                     CHISLON
                         During our conversations, you have 
                         talked of Summerdale... of a warlord 
                         that would one day save their world 
                         from the Ixis.  Did you know that I 
                         would one day exist?

                                     AZOIC
                         Do you dream of saving Neariah?  The 
                         warlord would have to be someone who 
                         could love nature's god.  I thought 
                         it might be you, Chislon.

                                     CHISLON
                         You are the only one who understands 
                         why I survived in this place.  I 
                         must meet Neariah.

                                     AZOIC
                         It seems this is your destiny.

                                     CHISLON
                         You must teach me what you can, Azoic.

                                     AZOIC
                         The gods may not approve.  Syntyche 
                         they can control.

                                     CHISLON
                         We must convince the gods once and 
                         for all.

               He abandons the oracle and rushes down the corridor.  Azoic 
               follows Chislon along a maze of identical corridors until he 
               veers through a pair of silently opening doors.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                                                        35.


               INT. VIRTUAL DOMINION - CONTINUOUS

               Azoic and Chislon step into a dizzying virtual recreation of 
               the oasis.  Disoriented, Azoic falters but Chislon moves 
               confidently through the floating vista.

               Azoic finally regains his balance, but stares emotionally at 
               the familiar kaleidoscope of images.

               Chislon is already wandering around the vista intently focused
